event = {
	id = 1000134
	random = no
	country = ger

	decision = {
		war = { country = ENG country = GER }
		war = { country = FRA country = GER }
     NOT = { war = { country = BEL country = GER } }
	   }

	decision_trigger = { 
		control = { province = 51 data = BEL } #布鲁塞尔
		control = { province = 56 data = FRA } #巴黎
		control = { province = 485 data = GER } #华沙
	        }
			
	trigger = {
		war = { country = ENG country = GER }
		war = { country = FRA country = GER }
		NOT = { war = { country = BEL country = GER }}
		control = { province = 51 data = BEL } #布鲁塞尔
		control = { province = 56 data = FRA } #巴黎
		control = { province = 485 data = GER } #华沙
	}

	name = "黄色方案：准备进攻西欧 "
	desc = "１９３９年９月，纳粹德国占领波兰之后，就对西欧虎视眈眈， 并开始策划进攻西欧诸国的作战计划。１０月９日，希特勒下达 了进攻西欧的第六号指令，德国陆军总司令部随即开始制定代号 为“黄色方案”的进攻计划，该计划实际上是第一次世界大战中 德军“施利芬计划”的翻版，即经比利时中部以法国巴黎为主要 突击方向。 "
	style = 0
	picture = "german_stratec_victory"

	date = { day = 2 month = october year = 1939 }
	offset = 7
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1940 }

	action_a = {
		name = "以施利芬计划为蓝本 "
		ai_chance = 98
		command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
		command = { type = resource which = money value = -50 }
		command = { type = setflag which = shilifen }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "直接采用曼斯坦因计划 "
		ai_chance = 2
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = resource which = money value = -200 }
		command = { type = setflag which = shilifen2 }
	}

	id = 1000143

	country = ger

		event = 1000134 #黄色方案

		control = { province = 51 data = BEL } #布鲁塞尔

		OR = {
			AND = {
				ai = no
				NOT = { war = { country = BEL country = GER }}
				year = 1940
				month = 4
			}
		    war = { country = BEL country = GER } #已经发生战争（手动或AI自动宣战）
